## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics (ODE rate laws for batch systems)
**Analysis**: The target dA_dt is the time-derivative of a chemical concentration A, indicating a kinetic rate law for how A changes in time t. With only (t, A) available, the most likely relationships are autonomous rate laws dA_dt = f(A) (reaction order, reversibility, autocatalysis) or explicitly time-dependent effective rate coefficients (activation/induction, deactivation, external forcing).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order decay: dA_dt = -c0 (constant-rate consumption; surface/zero-order regimes)
- First-order decay: dA_dt = -c0 * A (unimolecular decay or pseudo-first-order conditions)
- Second-order decay: dA_dt = -c0 * A**2 (bimolecular self-reaction 2A -> products)
- n-th order power-law: dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 (empirical overall reaction order / lumped kinetics)
- Linear relaxation to equilibrium: dA_dt = c0 * (c1 - A) (approach to a fixed point A=c1; pseudo-equilibrium / replenishment-consumption balance)
- Reversible first-order with conserved total: dA_dt = -c0 * A + c1 * (c2 - A) (A <-> B with A+B=c2; net drive toward equilibrium)
- Autocatalytic with depletion: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (self-accelerating at low A, slows near A≈c1 due to limitation)
- Competing growth/decay channels: dA_dt = c0 * A - c1 * A**2 - c2 * A (net = (c0-c2)A - c1*A**2; multiple parallel pathways lumped)
- Time-varying rate coefficient (deactivation/aging): dA_dt = -c0 * A * exp(-c1 * t) (effective first-order rate slows over time)
- Induction/activation period: dA_dt = -c0 * A * (1 - exp(-c1 * t)) (rate turns on gradually from ~0 to ~-c0*A)
- Fractal/heterogeneous kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 * t**c2 (non-ideal kinetics where apparent rate depends on time scale)
- Periodic forcing (feed/irradiation modulation): dA_dt = -c0 * A + c1 * sin(c2 * t) (externally driven source/sink with periodic component)
- Photochemical/self-shielding-like dependence on A: dA_dt = -c0 * exp(-c1 * A) (rate decreases with A due to attenuation or accessibility limits)
- Substrate/product inhibition (Haldane-type shape): dA_dt = -c0 * A / (c1 + A + c2 * A**2) (rate increases then decreases with A; inhibition at high A)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- If dA_dt is proportional to A (straight line in dA_dt vs A), it suggests pseudo-first-order kinetics; curvature in log(-dA_dt) vs log(A) indicates non-integer reaction order.
- A stable fixed point A* appears when dA_dt crosses zero; a factor like (c1 - A) indicates relaxation toward an equilibrium/steady concentration.
- Autocatalysis typically shows a positive dependence at low A and a limiting negative feedback at higher A, often captured by mixed linear and quadratic terms in A.
- Parallel reaction pathways often sum as additive sink terms (e.g., -c0*A - c1*A**2), producing composite curvature in dA_dt(A).
- Explicit exp(-c*t) multiplying a rate term indicates catalyst deactivation, fouling, or diminishing activity over time (slowing kinetics at later t).
- A (1 - exp(-c*t)) factor indicates induction/activation delays (slow start, then accelerating toward a steady kinetic regime).
- Power-law dependence on t (t**c) in the rate coefficient suggests transport limitation, aging media, or heterogeneous/fractal kinetics with scale dependence.
- Sinusoidal dependence on t points to external periodic driving (pulsed feed, light modulation, stirring cycles) rather than intrinsic chemistry alone.
- Rational inhibition forms with higher-order A in the denominator indicate self-inhibition/substrate inhibition, producing a peak reaction rate at intermediate A.

GT is the fixed function
\[
0.7991114344496316\,A^{1/3}\;-\;0.49947326957917104\,A\;-\;0.49947326957917104\,A\,e^{-0.050569865727257013\,t}.
\]
So any matching candidate must be exactly of the form
\[
(\alpha)A^{1/3}+(\beta)A+(\gamma)A e^{(\delta)t}
\]
with **no extra nonzero terms**, and with \(\delta=-0.0505698657\), \(\alpha=0.7991114344\), \(\beta=-0.4994732696\), \(\gamma=-0.4994732696\).

Below, for each candidate, I check whether all “extra” structures (sin/log/rational/etc.) can be zeroed out, and whether the remaining terms can be parameter-set to the GT.

---

### 1. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + A^{c4}c5\sin(c6 t+c7)\)
Set \(c5=0\) to remove the sine term. Then match by choosing:
- \(c0=0.7991114344496316\)
- \(c1=-0.49947326957917104\)
- \(c2=-0.49947326957917104\)
- \(c3=-0.050569865727257013\)
This becomes exactly GT. **Matches.**

### 2. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4 + c5\log(Ac6+1)\sin(c7 t+c8)\)
Set \(c4=0\) and \(c5=0\) to remove extra terms. Remaining three terms can be set as in (1). **Matches.**

### 3. \(Ac0 + Ac1 e^{c2 t} + A^{c3}c4 + c5 e^{Ac6} + c7 + c8\cos(Ac9)\)
To match GT we need an \(A^{1/3}\) term and no \(e^{A(\cdot)}\), cos, constants. You can zero \(c5,c8,c7\), but then you still need \(A^{c3}c4\) to be \(A^{1/3}\) (set \(c3=1/3\), \(c4=0.799...\)). However you also need a separate linear \(A\) term and an \(A e^{\delta t}\) term: those are \(Ac0\) and \(Ac1 e^{c2 t}\), OK. So far so good.
But note GT has **two** linear-in-\(A\) contributions: one plain \(A\) and one \(A e^{\delta t}\). Candidate has exactly those. So after setting \(c5=c8=c7=0\), it can match:
- \(c0=-0.49947326957917104\)
- \(c1=-0.49947326957917104\)
- \(c2=-0.050569865727257013\)
- \(c3=1/3\), \(c4=0.7991114344496316\)
Thus **matches**.

### 4. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4\log(c5 t+1)\)
Need no log term: set \(c4=0\). Then match remaining three terms as in (1). **Matches.**

### 5. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + A^{c4}c5\log(c6 t+1)\)
Remove last term by \(c5=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 6. \(Ac0 + \frac{Ac1}{A^2c2 + A + c3} + Ac4 e^{c5 t} + A^{c6}c7 + c8\)
GT has no rational-in-\(A\) term and no constant. Set \(c1=0\), \(c8=0\). Then need \(A^{c6}c7\) to be \(A^{1/3}\): set \(c6=1/3\), \(c7=0.799...\). Also need plain \(A\) term and \(A e^{\delta t}\): use \(Ac0\) and \(Ac4 e^{c5 t}\) with \(c0=-0.49947\), \(c4=-0.49947\), \(c5=-0.0505699\). **Matches.**

### 7. \(Ac0 + Ac1 e^{c2 t} + A^{c3}c4 e^{c5 t} + c6\log(Ac7+1) + c8\)
To avoid log and constant: set \(c6=0\), \(c8=0\). Remaining has an extra \(A^{c3}c4 e^{c5 t}\) term; GT has no \(A^{1/3}e^{(\cdot)t}\) term. Only way is set \(c4=0\) to remove it, but then you lose the needed \(A^{1/3}\) term entirely. So **cannot** match. **No match.**

### 8. \(Ac0 + Ac1 e^{c2 t} + A^{c3}c4 e^{c5 t} + c6 + c7\log(c8|A|+1)\)
Same issue as (7): to remove log/constant set \(c7=0\), \(c6=0\), but then still have \(A^{c3}c4 e^{c5 t}\) which must be removed (set \(c4=0\)), losing \(A^{1/3}\). **No match.**

### 9. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + \frac{Ac4}{A+c5} + A^{c6}c7 + c8\)
Need no \(A^2\), no rational, no constant: set \(c0=0\), \(c4=0\), \(c8=0\). Then set \(c6=1/3\), \(c7=0.799...\), and match \(c1,c2,c3\) to GT. **Matches.**

### 10. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + \frac{c4 t}{Ac5+c6} + \frac{c7}{Ac5+c6} + c8\)
Remove extra terms by \(c4=0\), \(c7=0\), \(c8=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 11. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4 t^{c5}\)
Remove extra term by \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 12. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + \frac{Ac4}{Ac5+c6} + \frac{c7}{Ac5+c6} + c8\)
Remove rational extras by \(c4=0\), \(c7=0\), \(c8=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 13. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 + Ac3 e^{c4 t} + Ac5 e^{c6 t} + c7\)
GT has only one exponential-in-\(t\) term and no standalone \(Ac2\) constant-in-\(t\) term, and no constant \(c7\). You can set \(c2=0\), \(c5=0\), \(c7=0\), leaving \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac3 e^{c4 t}\), which matches by choosing \(c3=-0.49947\), \(c4=-0.0505699\), etc. **Matches.**

### 14. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + Ac4 e^{c5 t} + c6\)
Need only one \(A e^{(\cdot)t}\) term and no constant: set \(c4=0\), \(c6=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 15. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4 e^{c5 t} + c6\)
Extra term \(c4 e^{c5 t}\) is not multiplied by \(A\) and GT has no such term; remove by \(c4=0\), also set \(c6=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 16. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4 + c5 t (A+c6)^{c7}\)
Remove extras by \(c4=0\), \(c5=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 17. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + \frac{Ac4}{c5 t+c6} + \frac{c7}{c5 t+c6}\)
Extra rational-in-\(t\) terms must vanish: set \(c4=0\), \(c7=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 18. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4 t^{c5} + c6\)
Set \(c4=0\), \(c6=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 19. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + Ac4(c5+t)^{c6} + c7\)
Need no extra \(A\cdot (c5+t)^{c6}\) term and no constant: set \(c4=0\), \(c7=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 20. \(Ac0 + Ac1 e^{c2 t} + A^{c3}c4 e^{c5 t} + c6\)
To get \(A^{1/3}\) term, you’d use \(A^{c3}c4 e^{c5 t}\), but that introduces \(t\)-dependence unless \(c5=0\). If set \(c5=0\), term becomes \(A^{c3}c4\) which can be \(A^{1/3}\). Also must remove constant: \(c6=0\). Then match:
- \(c0=-0.49947\)
- \(c1=-0.49947\), \(c2=-0.0505699\)
- \(c3=1/3\), \(c4=0.7991114\)
**Matches.**

### 21. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4\log(Ac5 + c6 e^{c7 t} + 1)\)
GT has no log term; remove by \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 22. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + \frac{Ac2}{A+c3} + Ac4 e^{c5 t} + c6\)
Remove rational and constant: set \(c2=0\), \(c6=0\). Then you have \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac4 e^{c5 t}\), which matches by setting \(c4=-0.49947\), \(c5=-0.0505699\), etc. **Matches.**

### 23. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4 e^{Ac5} + c6\)
Remove \(e^{A(\cdot)}\) and constant: set \(c4=0\), \(c6=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 24. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4 e^{c5 t}\)
Remove extra exponential term by \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 25. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4 + c5 t\)
Remove extra affine-in-\(t\) terms by \(c4=0\), \(c5=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 26. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4 t (A+c5)^{c6}\)
Remove extra term by \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 27. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4\sin(Ac5+c6) + c7\)
Remove sine and constant by \(c4=0\), \(c7=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 28. \(Ac0 + Ac1 e^{c2 t} + \frac{Ac3}{A+c4} + A^{c5}c6 + c7\)
Remove rational and constant: set \(c3=0\), \(c7=0\). Set \(c5=1/3\), \(c6=0.799...\). Match \(c0,c1,c2\) to GT. **Matches.**

### 29. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + Ac4 e^{c5 t}\)
Remove extra \(A e^{c5 t}\) by \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 30. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 + Ac3 e^{c4 t} + Ac5 e^{c6 t}\)
Set \(c2=0\), \(c5=0\). Then match \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac3 e^{c4 t}\) to GT. **Matches.**

### 31. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + \frac{c4 t}{Ac5+c6} + \frac{c7}{Ac5+c6}\)
Set \(c4=0\), \(c7=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 32. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + \frac{Ac4}{Ac5+c6} + \frac{c7}{Ac5+c6}\)
Set \(c4=0\), \(c7=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 33. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + Ac4 + c5\)
GT has no extra \(Ac4\) beyond the existing \(Ac1\), and no constant. Set \(c4=0\), \(c5=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 34. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 + Ac3 + Ac4 e^{c5 t} + c6\)
Combine \(Ac1+Ac2+Ac3\) into one linear \(A\) coefficient by setting \(c2=0,c3=0\) (or any combination). Remove constant \(c6=0\). Then match \(Ac4 e^{c5 t}\) to the exponential term and \(Ac1\) to the plain \(A\) term, plus \(A^{1/3}c0\). **Matches.**

### 35. \(Ac0 + Ac1 e^{c2 t} + c3|A|^{1/3} + c4\)
GT uses \(A^{1/3}\), not \(|A|^{1/3}\). Unless the domain is restricted to \(A\ge 0\) (not allowed here), \(|A|^{1/3}\neq A^{1/3}\) for negative \(A\). You can’t fix that with constants. Setting \(c3=0\) removes it but then you lose the needed \(A^{1/3}\) term. **No match.**

### 36. \(Ac0 + Ac1 e^{c2 t} + A^{c3}c4 + c5\)
Set \(c5=0\). Set \(c3=1/3\), \(c4=0.799...\). Match \(c0,c1,c2\) to GT. **Matches.**

### 37. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4\)
Set \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 38. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4 + c5\sin(c6\log(Ac7+1)+c8)\)
Set \(c4=0\), \(c5=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 39. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4 e^{Ac5}\cos(c6 t)\)
Remove last term by \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 40. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4\sin(Ac5+c6)\)
Set \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 41. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4 + c5\log(c6 e^{Ac7}+1)\)
Set \(c4=0\), \(c5=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 42. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 + Ac3 e^{c4 t}\)
Set \(c2=0\). Then match \(Ac1\) to plain \(A\), and \(Ac3 e^{c4 t}\) to exponential term. **Matches.**

### 43. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t}\)
Directly the same structure as GT; set \(c0,c1,c2,c3\) to the GT coefficients/exponent. **Matches.**

### 44. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4 e^{c5 t}\log(Ac6+1)\)
Remove extra term by \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 45. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + Ac4(c5+t)^{c6}\)
Set \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 46. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4\sin(c5\log(Ac6+1)+c7)\)
Set \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 47. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + A^{c4}c5\)
Need no extra power term; set \(c5=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 48. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4\log(c5 t+1) + c6\)
Set \(c4=0\), \(c6=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 49. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + \frac{Ac2}{A^2c3 + A + c4} + Ac5 e^{c6 t}\)
Remove rational by \(c2=0\). Then match \(Ac5 e^{c6 t}\) to exponential term and \(Ac1\) to plain \(A\). **Matches.**

### 50. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + \frac{Ac2}{A+c3} + Ac4 e^{c5 t}\)
Set \(c2=0\). Then match remaining terms. **Matches.**

### 51. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + A^{c4}c5 + c6\)
Set \(c5=0\), \(c6=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 52. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4 e^{Ac5} e^{c6 t}\)
Remove extra term by \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 53. \(Ac0 + Ac1 e^{c2 t} + A^{c3}c4 + c5\log(Ac6+1) + c7\)
Set \(c5=0\), \(c7=0\). Set \(c3=1/3\), \(c4=0.799...\). Match \(c0,c1,c2\). **Matches.**

### 54. \(Ac0 + Ac1 e^{c2 t} + A^{c3}c4 + c5 + c6\log(c7|A|+1)\)
To avoid \(|A|\) log and constant: set \(c6=0\), \(c5=0\). Then set \(c3=1/3\), \(c4=0.799...\), and match \(c0,c1,c2\). **Matches.**

### 55. \(Ac0 + Ac1 e^{c2 t} + c3|A|^{c4} + c5 + c6\log(c7|A|+1)\)
If keep \(|A|^{c4}\) to represent \(A^{1/3}\), impossible for negative \(A\). If set it to zero (e.g., \(c3=0\)), then no \(A^{1/3}\) term remains. So **no match**.

### 56. \(Ac0 + Ac1 e^{c2 t} + c3|A|^{1/3} + c4 + c5\log(c6|A|+1)\)
Same absolute-value obstruction: to match GT for all real \(A\), cannot use \(|A|^{1/3}\). Setting \(c3=0\) removes needed term. **No match.**

### 57. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4\log(Ac5+1) + c6\)
Set \(c4=0\), \(c6=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 58. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4 + c5\log(c6|A|+1)\)
Set \(c5=0\), \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 59. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + Ac2 + Ac3 e^{c4 t} + c5\)
Remove \(A^2\) and constant: set \(c1=0\), \(c5=0\). Then match \(Ac2\) to plain \(A\) and \(Ac3 e^{c4 t}\) to exponential term. **Matches.**

### 60. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + Ac2 + Ac3 + Ac4 e^{c5 t} + c6\)
Set \(c1=0\), \(c3=0\), \(c6=0\). Then match remaining. **Matches.**

### 61. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4 e^{Ac5}\)
Set \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 62. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4\log(Ac5+1)\)
Set \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 63. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^{1/3}c1\log(c2 t+1) + Ac3 + Ac4 e^{c5 t} + c6\)
GT has no \(A^{1/3}\log(\cdot)\) and no constant: set \(c1=0\), \(c6=0\). Then match \(Ac3\) and \(Ac4 e^{c5 t}\) and \(A^{1/3}c0\). **Matches.**

### 64. \(Ac0 + Ac1 e^{c2 t} + A^{c3}c4 + c5 e^{Ac6} + c7\)
Set \(c5=0\), \(c7=0\). Set \(c3=1/3\), \(c4=0.799...\). Match \(c0,c1,c2\). **Matches.**

### 65. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4\log(c5 e^{Ac6}+1)\)
Remove log term by \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 66. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + \frac{c4 t}{c5 t+c6} + \frac{c7}{c5 t+c6} + c8\)
Set \(c4=0\), \(c7=0\), \(c8=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 67. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + \frac{c4 t}{c5 t+c6} + \frac{c7}{c5 t+c6}\)
Set \(c4=0\), \(c7=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 68. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4\exp(c5\sin(c6\log(c7|A|+c8 t+1)+c9))\)
Extra complicated term must be removed: set \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 69. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + Ac2 + Ac3 e^{c4 t}\)
Set \(c1=0\). Then match \(Ac2\) and \(Ac3 e^{c4 t}\) and \(A^{1/3}c0\). **Matches.**

### 70. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + Ac2 + Ac3 + Ac4 e^{c5 t}\)
Set \(c1=0\), \(c3=0\). Then match remaining. **Matches.**

### 71. \(Ac0 + Ac1 e^{c2 t} + \frac{A^{c3}c4}{A^{c3}+c5} + c6\)
The fraction term is not a pure power \(A^{1/3}\); it tends to \(c4\) for large \(A\) (if \(c5\neq 0\)) and is not proportional to \(A^{1/3}\) for all \(A\). If set \(c5=0\), it becomes constant \(c4\), not \(A^{1/3}\). Only way is set \(c4=0\) to remove it, but then no \(A^{1/3}\) term exists. **No match.**

### 72. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + A^{c4}c5 e^{c6 t} + c7\)
Remove extra term and constant by \(c5=0\), \(c7=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 73. \(Ac0 + Ac1 e^{c2 t} + \frac{A^{c3}c4}{A^{c3}+c5} + c6 e^{Ac7} + c8\)
As in (71), the fraction cannot produce \(A^{1/3}\); setting it to zero removes needed term. Also can remove \(e^{A(\cdot)}\) by \(c6=0\), constant by \(c8=0\), but still no \(A^{1/3}\). **No match.**

### 74. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + \frac{Ac4}{A+c5} + \frac{A^{c6}c7}{A^{c6}+c8} + c9\)
The last fraction cannot equal \(0.799A^{1/3}\) for all \(A\) (same saturation issue). If set \(c7=0\) to remove it, then no \(A^{1/3}\) term remains (other terms are \(A^2\), \(A\), \(Ae^{...}\), rational-in-\(A\), constant). So **no match.**

### 75. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4 + c5\log(c6 e^{Ac7 + c8 t}+1)\)
Set \(c5=0\), \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 76. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4 + c5 e^{c6\sin(c7 t+c8)}\)
Set \(c5=0\), \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 77. \(Ac0 + Ac1 e^{c2 t} + \frac{A^{c3}c4}{A^{c3}+c5} + c6\log(Ac7+1) + c8\)
Remove log and constant by \(c6=0\), \(c8=0\). Still fraction cannot yield \(A^{1/3}\); removing it loses needed term. **No match.**

### 78. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4 + c5 e^{c6 t}\log(Ac7+1)\)
Set \(c5=0\), \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 79. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4\sin(c5+c6 t)\)
Set \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 80. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + \frac{Ac4}{c5 t+c6} + c7 + \frac{c8}{c5 t+c6}\)
Set \(c4=0\), \(c7=0\), \(c8=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 81. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4 + c5\sin(c6 t+c7)\)
Set \(c4=0\), \(c5=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 82. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + \frac{A^{c4}c5}{A^{c4}+c6} + c7\)
The fraction term cannot equal a pure \(A^{1/3}\) (it saturates). If set \(c5=0\) to remove it, then you still have \(A^{1/3}c0\) already, so that’s fine; also set \(c7=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 83. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + Ac4\sin(c5 t+c6) + c7\)
Set \(c4=0\), \(c7=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 84. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4 e^{c5\sin(c6 t+c7)}\)
Set \(c4=0\). Then match first three terms. **Matches.**

### 85. \(Ac0 + Ac1 e^{c2 t} + c3\log(Ac4+1) + c5 + c6\sin(c7\log(Ac8+1)+c9)\)
To match GT, must remove log/sin/constant: set \(c3=0\), \(c6=0\), \(c5=0\). Then remaining is \(Ac0 + Ac1 e^{c2 t}\) with no \(A^{1/3}\) term. So **no match.**

### 86. \(Ac0 + Ac1 e^{c2 t} + c3 + c4\log(c5|A|+1) + c6\sin(c7\log(c8|A|+1)+c9)\)
Removing extras by \(c4=0\), \(c6=0\), \(c3=0\) leaves no \(A^{1/3}\). Keeping \(|A|\)-log doesn’t help. **No match.**

### 87. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + \frac{Ac4}{A+c5} + \frac{Ac6\log(Ac7+1)}{A+c8} + c9\)
No \(A^{1/3}\) term exists anywhere. Cannot create it by parameter choice. **No match.**

### 88. \(Ac0 + \frac{Ac1}{A^2c2 + A + c3} + Ac4 e^{c5 t} + \frac{Ac6}{A^2c7 + A + c8} + c9\)
